<p begin="29270074166t" end="29296767499t" region="region_1" xml:id="subtitle854"><span style="style_3">We change it up. We morph. We adapt.</span></p>
<p begin="29297601666t" end="29309697082t" region="region_1" xml:id="subtitle855"><span style="style_3">We all have our--</span></p>
<p begin="29310531249t" end="29357244582t" region="region_1" xml:id="subtitle856"><span style="style_3">For example, we all have</span><br/><span style="style_3">our “trying to get a good job” voice.</span></p>
<p begin="29364752082t" end="29396033332t" region="region_1" xml:id="subtitle857"><span style="style_3">When you walk in for that interview,</span><br/><span style="style_3">you don’t sound the way you sound</span></p>
<p begin="29396867499t" end="29420641249t" region="region_1" xml:id="subtitle858"><span style="style_3">on a Saturday night</span><br/><span style="style_3">when you’re having a couple drinks.</span></p>
<p begin="29421475416t" end="29446083332t" region="region_1" xml:id="subtitle859"><span style="style_3">You clean it up. You practice in the car.</span></p>
<p begin="29446917499t" end="29465269166t" region="region_1" xml:id="subtitle860"><span style="style_3">And when you walk in, you turn it on.</span></p>
<p begin="29466103332t" end="29480701249t" region="region_1" xml:id="subtitle861"><span style="style_3">“If you’ll check my references,</span></p>
<p begin="29481535416t" end="29502806666t" region="region_1" xml:id="subtitle862"><span style="style_3">you’ll see I’m more than qualified</span><br/><span style="style_3">for this position.</span></p>
<p begin="29503640832t" end="29518655832t" region="region_1" xml:id="subtitle863"><span style="style_3">Please feel free to call Frank Torres.</span></p>

<p begin="40532158332t" end="40563856666t" region="region_1" xml:id="subtitle1213"><span style="style_3">Basically, Martin and I are doing a show</span><br/><span style="style_3">in Sacramento, California.</span></p>

<p begin="43884674166t" end="43908030832t" region="region_1" xml:id="subtitle1333"><span style="style_3">Now keep in mind this area is full.</span></p>
<p begin="43908865000t" end="43935975416t" region="region_1" xml:id="subtitle1334"><span style="style_3">In Mobile</span><br/><span style="style_3">the aisle was right up the middle.</span></p>
